 200: def parse_page_selector(page_selector: str, page_count: int) -> list[int]:  # 设计：解析页码选择器；功能：展开范围并校验边界；默认超范围和超量即报错，原因：保护上下文体积。
 201:     if not page_selector.strip():
 202:         raise ValueError("Page selector cannot be empty.")
 203: 
 204:     normalized = (
 205:         page_selector.replace("，", ",")
 206:         .replace("；", ",")
 207:         .replace("、", ",")
 208:         .replace("~", "-")
 209:         .replace("～", "-")
 210:         .replace(":", "-")
 211:         .replace("：", "-")
 212:     )
 213: 
 214:     pages: set[int] = set()
 215:     for part in normalized.split(","):
 216:         chunk = part.strip()
 217:         if not chunk:
 218:             continue
 219: 
 220:         if "-" in chunk:
 221:             start_str, end_str = chunk.split("-", 1)
 222:             start_page = int(start_str)
 223:             end_page = int(end_str)
 224:             if start_page > end_page:
 225:                 start_page, end_page = end_page, start_page
 226:             pages.update(range(start_page, end_page + 1))
 227:             continue
 228: 
 229:         pages.add(int(chunk))
 230: 
 231:     if not pages:
 232:         raise ValueError("No valid pages were parsed from the selector.")
 233: 
 234:     invalid_pages = sorted(page for page in pages if page < 1 or page > page_count)
 235:     if invalid_pages:
 236:         raise ValueError(
 237:             f"Pages out of range: {invalid_pages}. The PDF has {page_count} pages."
 238:         )
 239: 
 240:     selected_pages = sorted(pages)
 241:     if len(selected_pages) > MAX_TOOL_PAGE_READ:
 242:         raise ValueError(
 243:             f"Too many pages requested at once ({len(selected_pages)}). "
 244:             f"Please narrow the selection to {MAX_TOOL_PAGE_READ} pages or fewer."
 245:         )
 246: 
 247:     return selected_pages
 248: 
 249: 
 250: def format_pdf_pages_for_agent(pdf_file_path: str | Path, page_numbers: list[int]) -> str:  # 设计：统一渲染读页结果；功能：按 [Page N] 拼多页文本；默认无文本页给占位说明，原因：避免误判为空返回。
 251:     pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_file_path)
 252:     rendered_pages: list[str] = []
 253:     for page_number in page_numbers:
 254:         page_text = pages[page_number - 1]
 255:         if not page_text:
 256:             page_text = "[No extractable text found on this page. It may be image-only or scanned.]"
 257:         rendered_pages.append(f"[Page {page_number}]\n{page_text}")
 258:     return "\n\n".join(rendered_pages)

 261: class ReadPdfPageIndexTool(BaseTool):  # 设计：提供筛页工具；功能：返回当前 PDF 页索引；默认要求先读索引再读页，原因：减少无关页加载。
 262:     name: str = "Step 1 - Read PDF Page Index"
 263:     description: str = (
 264:         "Read the current PDF page index JSON. Always call this first before reading any PDF page."
 265:         "Use the page-by-page topic list to decide which exact pages are relevant to the current task."

 269:     def _run(self, keyword: str = "", max_results: int = 0) -> str:  # 设计：执行索引读取；功能：按条件返回 JSON 文本；可调：keyword、max_results；默认空值返回全量，原因：兼容最简单调用。

 273: 
 274:         if keyword:
 275:             lowered_keyword = keyword.lower().strip()

 278:                 for page in pages
 279:                 if lowered_keyword in str(page.get("topic", "")).lower()
 280:                 or lowered_keyword in str(page.get("page_number", ""))
 281:             ]

 289:             "page_count": index_data.get("page_count", len(pages)),
 290:             "pages": pages,
 291:         }

  68:         normalized = ""
  69:     if not normalized:

  75:         cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
  76:         if len(cleaned) >= 2:
  77:             return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
  78:     return fallback

  82:     if not cleaned:
  83:         return ""
  84: 
  85:     if cleaned.startswith("```"):

  87:         if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
  88:             cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()
  89:

  91:         data = json.loads(cleaned)
  92:     except Exception:
  93:         return cleaned
  94:

  97:     return ""
  98: 
  99: def build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 设计：集中组装单页 prompt；功能：拼规则、页码和页文；默认 company_name 为空，原因：兼容上游未识别公司名。

 119:     return Agent(
 120:         role=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,  # 默认“PDF 逐页索引专员”；可改成更贴近你内部角色定义的名字。
 121:         goal=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,  # 默认聚焦“逐页筛页”；可改成更强调招股书目录化摘要。
 122:         backstory=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,  # 默认强调“不跨页总结”；可按文档类型微调语境。
 123:         llm=get_llm(
 124:             temperature=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
 125:             timeout=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 126:             max_retries=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
 127:         ),
 128:         verbose=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
 129:         allow_delegation=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ALLOW_DELEGATION,
 130:         reasoning=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_REASONING,
 131:         cache=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_CACHE,
 132:         max_retry_limit=PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_MAX_RETRIES,
 133:     )
 134: 
 135: """页索引执行"""
 136: 
 137: def summarize_page_topic(  # 设计：执行单页打标；功能：返回页码与主题映射；可调：company_name 可传空串；默认空页直返固定标签，原因：避免无效调用。
 138:     agent: Agent,
 139:     page_number: int,
 140:     page_text: str,
 141:     company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；上游识别出公司名时传入可提升主题稳定性。
 142: ) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
 143:     fallback = PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
 144:     if not page_text.strip():
 145:         return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
 146: 
 147:     prompt = build_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number=page_number, page_text=page_text, company_name=company_name)
 148:     started_at = perf_counter()
 149: 
 150:     try:
 151:         result = agent.kickoff(prompt, response_format=PageTopicSummary)
 152:         topic = ""
 153:         if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
 154:             topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
 155:         if not topic:
 156:             topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
 157:         elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 158:         print(f"[PDF Index] page {page_number} completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s")
 159:     except Exception as exc:
 160:         elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 161:         print(
 162:             "[PDF Index] page "
 163:             f"{page_number} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
 164:             f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 165:         )
 166:         topic = _heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback)
 167: 
 168:     return PdfPageIndexEntry(
 169:         page_number=page_number,
 170:         topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
 171:     )
 172: 
 173: """页索引入口"""
 174: 
 175: def ensure_pdf_page_index(  # 设计：页索引总入口；功能：优先读缓存再按需重建；可调：company_name、force_rebuild；默认空公司名且不强制重建，原因：兼容性更高。
 176:     pdf_file_path: str,
 177:     company_name: str = "",  # 默认空字符串；传入公司名可让逐页主题标注更贴近业务语境。
 178:     force_rebuild: bool = PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,  # 默认 False；改 True 时忽略缓存，强制重建整本索引。
 179: ) -> str:
 180:     pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
 181:     if not pdf_path.exists():
 182:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")
 183: 
 184:     index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
 185:     if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
 186:         set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
 187:         return str(index_path)
 188: 
 189:     pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
 190:     page_indexer = create_page_indexer_agent()
 191:     page_entries: list[PdfPageIndexEntry] = []
 192: 
 193:     for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1):
 194:         print(f"[PDF Index] summarizing page {page_number}/{len(pages)}")
 195:         page_entries.append(
 196:             summarize_page_topic(
 197:                 agent=page_indexer,
 198:                 page_number=page_number,
 199:                 page_text=page_text,
 200:                 company_name=company_name,
 201:             )
 202:         )
 203: 
 204:     payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
 205:     saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
 206:     set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
 207:     return saved_index_path
 208: 
 209: 
 210: """运行态清理"""
 211: 
 212: def reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 设计：清理预处理运行态；功能：只清进程内缓存；默认保留磁盘缓存，原因：复跑更快。
 213:     reset_pdf_page_tool_runtime_state()
 214: 
 215: 
 216: def reset_pdf_indexing_runtime_state() -> None:  # 设计：兼容旧入口；功能：转调新清理函数；默认仅做别名保留，原因：避免旧代码失效。
 217:     reset_pdf_preprocessing_runtime_state()

### 0025 ASSISTANT (final_answer)

```text
它的实现意图可以概括成一句话：先把整份 PDF 预处理成“按页主题索引”，让后续 agent 不用盲读整本，只先看每页标签，再精读相关页。

**整体意图**

[`pdf_indexing_parellel.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py#L288) 的入口 `ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel()` 会先检查已有页索引缓存是否还能复用；如果能复用，就直接设置当前 PDF 上下文并返回索引路径。如果不能，就抽取整本 PDF 的页文本，给每一页生成一个很短的 `topic` 标签，最后把这些标签保存成 JSON 索引。

这个索引真正服务的是 [`pdf_page_tools.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/tools/pdf_page_tools.py#L261) 里的两个工具：先读页索引，再按需读具体页。也就是说，它不是为了“总结 PDF”，而是为了“缩小后续阅读范围”。

**主流程**

[`extract_pdf_pages()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/tools/pdf_page_tools.py#L118) 负责用 `fitz` 把 PDF 按页抽成文本，并做进程内缓存。

[`summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py#L268) 会为每一页创建异步任务，但用 `Semaphore` 控制并发上限，避免一次把 LLM 打爆。

[`summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py#L386) 的目标非常窄：只看当前页，输出一个极短 `topic`。它还做了几层兜底：空白页直接返回默认标签，模型报错时按关键字判断是否重试，最终失败就从页内第一条像标题的文本里猜一个主题。

[`build_page_index_payload()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/tools/pdf_page_tools.py#L137) 和 [`save_page_index()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/tools/pdf_page_tools.py#L153) 会把结果落盘成 JSON，并带上 fingerprint，这样下次可以靠 [`page_index_is_current()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/tools/pdf_page_tools.py#L184) 判断缓存是否过期。

**和串行版的区别**

相比 [`pdf_indexing.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing.py#L175)，这个文件最大的区别是把“逐页调用 Agent”换成了“受限并发的 LiteAgent 异步调用”。

它想解决的核心问题是：整本 PDF 页数多时，串行逐页打标太慢；但又不能无脑全并发，所以用了“并发上限 + 可重试 + 快速失败 + heuristics 兜底”的组合。

**我额外注意到的一点**

这个文件里前半段有一份乱码版定义，后半段又用 ASCII 重新定义了一遍同名常量、类和函数，比如 [`build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py#L348) 和 [`summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async()`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py#L386)。实际运行时以后面这份为准，所以作者的意图很明显是“保留功能，覆盖编码漂移”，但这个文件现在可读性比较差，后续最好清理成单份实现。

如果你愿意，我下一步可以继续帮你把这个文件画成一张“调用链/数据流”图，或者直接对比它和串行版哪些地方值得保留、哪些地方该重构。
```

Exit code: 0

Output:
from __future__ import annotations

import asyncio
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from time import perf_counter

from crewai.lite_agent import LiteAgent
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.crew import get_llm
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.pdf_page_tools import (
    PdfPageIndexEntry,
    build_page_index_payload,
    default_page_index_path,
    extract_pdf_pages,
    page_index_is_current,
    save_page_index,
    set_pdf_context,
)

"""并发版 PDF 逐页索引"""

"""并发页索引 Agent 参数"""

PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 并发逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；功能：限定 agent 只做逐页打标；原因：避免提前跨页分析。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；功能：为后续 agent 提供筛页标签；原因：减少全文盲读。
    "并发读取 PDF 页面，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速定位相关页。"
)
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景；功能：强化单页视角；原因：防止越界总结整份文档。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 可调：常用 0-0.3；默认 0.1，原因：标签更稳更短。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = False  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因：并发执行时避免日志过多。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 可调：建议 >0；默认 20，原因：单页调用不应长时间阻塞。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 可调：建议 1-8；默认 4，原因：在吞吐和限流风险之间折中。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 可调：建议 >=0；默认 2，原因：预处理容忍短暂波动但不无限重试。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 可调：建议 >0；默认 2 秒，原因：给限流或瞬时故障留恢复时间。

"""并发页索引任务参数"""

PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 可调：建议 4-15；默认 10，原因：既短又够区分主题。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位；功能：补齐 prompt 上下文；原因：上游可能识别失败。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；功能：显式标记无文本页；原因：避免误判异常。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因：优先复用缓存。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认规则集；功能：约束标签长度和口径；原因：后续筛页更稳定。
    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)


class ParallelPageTopicSummary(BaseModel):  # 设计：定义单页结构化输出；功能：只保留 topic；默认最小字段集便于稳定解析。
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")


"""并发页索引辅助函数"""


def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：统一清洗主题；功能：压成稳定短标签；默认超长截断且空值回退，原因：便于筛页与展示。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：兜底生成主题；功能：失败时取首个像标题的文本；默认回退 fallback，原因：索引流程不能中断。
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 设计：兼容兜底解析；功能：从 raw 中提取 topic；默认异常时返回原文或空串，原因：后续还会再清洗。
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 设计：统一解析 LiteAgent 输出；功能：优先读结构化字段，失败再读 raw；原因：兼容不同返回形态。
    topic = ""
    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
    if not topic:
        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
    return topic


def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 设计：读取整型环境变量；功能：给并发和重试参数留运行时开关；默认非法值回退默认值，原因：减少配置错误影响。
    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default

    try:
        return max(minimum, int(raw))
    except ValueError:
        return default


def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 设计：暴露并发度配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于部署侧调优。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
        minimum=1,
    )


def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 设计：暴露重试次数配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于按模型稳定性调优。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
        minimum=0,
    )


def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 设计：识别可重试错误；功能：只对限流和临时故障重试；原因：避免对确定性错误无意义重放。
    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
    retryable_markers = (
        "429",
        "rate limit",
        "too many requests",
        "timeout",
        "timed out",
        "connection",
        "temporarily unavailable",
        "bad gateway",
        "gateway timeout",
        "service unavailable",
        "502",
        "503",
        "504",
    )
    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)


def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 设计：集中组装单页 prompt；功能：拼规则、页码和页文；默认 company_name 为空，原因：兼容上游未识别公司名。
    prompt_parts = [
        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
        "",
        "规则：",
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"公司名称：{company_name or PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"页码：{page_number}",
            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


"""并发页索引 Agent"""


def create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent() -> LiteAgent:  # 设计：独立创建并发索引 agent；功能：为每个异步任务提供轻量单页执行器；默认快失败配置，原因：预处理应尽快回退。
    return LiteAgent(
        role=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,
        goal=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,
        backstory=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=0,
        ),
        verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
        max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
        response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
    )


"""并发页索引执行"""


async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(  # 设计：执行单页异步打标；功能：返回页码与主题映射；默认空页直返固定标签，原因：避免无效调用。
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str,
    total_pages: int,
    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
        page_number=page_number,
        page_text=page_text,
        company_name=company_name,
    )
    retry_limit = get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit()

    async with semaphore:
        for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
            started_at = perf_counter()
            try:
                result = await create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent().kickoff_async(
                    prompt,
                    response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
                )
                topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                print(
                    f"[PDF Index Parallel] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
                    f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )
            except Exception as exc:
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
                if should_retry:
                    delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
                    print(
                        "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
                        f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
                    )
                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
                    continue

                print(
                    "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
                )

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)


async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(  # 设计：并发执行整本 PDF 打标；功能：受限并发汇总全部页结果；默认保持页序，原因：便于直接落盘成索引。
    pages: list[str],
    company_name: str = "",
    max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
    total_pages = len(pages)
    tasks = [
        summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
            page_number=page_number,
            page_text=page_text,
            company_name=company_name,
            total_pages=total_pages,
            semaphore=semaphore,
        )
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
    ]
    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)


"""并发页索引入口"""


def ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel(  # 设计：并发页索引总入口；功能：优先读缓存再按需重建；可调：company_name、force_rebuild；默认空公司名且不强制重建，原因：兼容性更高。
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",
    force_rebuild: bool = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
    max_concurrency = get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency()
    print(
        "[PDF Index Parallel] using bounded concurrency "
        f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
    )
    page_entries = asyncio.run(
        summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
            pages=pages,
            company_name=company_name,
            max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
        )
    )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
    return saved_index_path
```

  66: def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：统一清洗主题；功能：压成稳定短标签；默认超长截断且空值回退，原因：便于筛页与展示。
  67:     normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
  68:     normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
  69:     compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
  70:     if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
  71:         normalized = ""
  72:     if not normalized:
  73:         normalized = fallback
  74:     return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]
  75: 
  76: 
  77: def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：兜底生成主题；功能：失败时取首个像标题的文本；默认回退 fallback，原因：索引流程不能中断。
  78:     for line in page_text.splitlines():
  79:         cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
  80:         if len(cleaned) >= 2:
  81:             return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
  82:     return fallback
  83: 
  84: 
  85: def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 设计：兼容兜底解析；功能：从 raw 中提取 topic；默认异常时返回原文或空串，原因：后续还会再清洗。
  86:     cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
  87:     if not cleaned:
  88:         return ""
  89: 
  90:     if cleaned.startswith("```"):
  91:         cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
  92:         if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
  93:             cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()
  94: 
  95:     try:
  96:         data = json.loads(cleaned)
  97:     except Exception:
  98:         return cleaned
  99: 
 100:     if isinstance(data, dict):
 101:         return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
 102:     return ""
 103:

 105: def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 设计：统一解析 LiteAgent 输出；功能：优先读结构化字段，失败再读 raw；原因：兼容不同返回形态。
 106:     topic = ""
 107:     if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
 108:         topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
 109:     if not topic:
 110:         topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
 111:     return topic
 112: 
 113: 
 114: def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 设计：读取整型环境变量；功能：给并发和重试参数留运行时开关；默认非法值回退默认值，原因：减少配置错误影响。
 115:     raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
 116:     if not raw:
 117:         return default
 118: 
 119:     try:
 120:         return max(minimum, int(raw))
 121:     except ValueError:
 122:         return default
 123: 
 124: 
 125: def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 设计：暴露并发度配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于部署侧调优。
 126:     return _read_int_env(
 127:         "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
 128:         PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,

 130:     )
 131: 
 132: 
 133: def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 设计：暴露重试次数配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于按模型稳定性调优。
 134:     return _read_int_env(
 135:         "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
 136:         PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
 137:         minimum=0,
 138:     )
 139: 
 140: 
 141: def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 设计：识别可重试错误；功能：只对限流和临时故障重试；原因：避免对确定性错误无意义重放。
 142:     error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
 143:     retryable_markers = (
 144:         "429",
 145:         "rate limit",
 146:         "too many requests",
 147:         "timeout",
 148:         "timed out",
 149:         "connection",
 150:         "temporarily unavailable",
 151:         "bad gateway",
 152:         "gateway timeout",
 153:         "service unavailable",
 154:         "502",
 155:         "503",
 156:         "504",
 157:     )
 158:     return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)
 159: 
 160: 
 161: def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 设计：集中组装单页 prompt；功能：拼规则、页码和页文；默认 company_name 为空，原因：兼容上游未识别公司名。
 162:     prompt_parts = [
 163:         "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
 164:         "",
 165:         "规则：",
 166:     ]
 167:     prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
 168:     prompt_parts.extend(
 169:         [
 170:             "",
 171:             f"公司名称：{company_name or PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
 172:             f"页码：{page_number}",
 173:             f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
 174:         ]
 175:     )
 176:     return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()
 177: 
 178: 
 179: """并发页索引 Agent"""
 180: 
 181: 
 182: def create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent() -> LiteAgent:  # 设计：独立创建并发索引 agent；功能：为每个异步任务提供轻量单页执行器；默认快失败配置，原因：预处理应尽快回退。
 183:     return LiteAgent(
 184:         role=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,
 185:         goal=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,
 186:         backstory=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,
 187:         llm=get_llm(
 188:             temperature=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
 189:             timeout=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 190:             max_retries=0,
 191:         ),
 192:         verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
 193:         max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 194:         response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
 195:     )
 196: 
 197: 
 198: """并发页索引执行"""
 199: 
 200: 
 201: async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(  # 设计：执行单页异步打标；功能：返回页码与主题映射；默认空页直返固定标签，原因：避免无效调用。
 202:     page_number: int,
 203:     page_text: str,
 204:     company_name: str,
 205:     total_pages: int,
 206:     semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
 207: ) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
 208:     fallback = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
 209:     if not page_text.strip():
 210:         return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
 211: 
 212:     prompt = build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
 213:         page_number=page_number,
 214:         page_text=page_text,
 215:         company_name=company_name,
 216:     )
 217:     retry_limit = get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit()
 218: 
 219:     async with semaphore:
 220:         for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
 221:             started_at = perf_counter()
 222:             try:
 223:                 result = await create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent().kickoff_async(
 224:                     prompt,
 225:                     response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
 226:                 )
 227:                 topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
 228:                 elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 229:                 print(
 230:                     f"[PDF Index Parallel] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
 231:                     f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
 232:                 )
 233:                 return PdfPageIndexEntry(
 234:                     page_number=page_number,
 235:                     topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
 236:                 )
 237:             except Exception as exc:
 238:                 elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 239:                 should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
 240:                 if should_retry:
 241:                     delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
 242:                     print(
 243:                         "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
 244:                         f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
 245:                         f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
 246:                         f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
 247:                         f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
 248:                     )
 249:                     await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
 250:                     continue
 251: 
 252:                 print(
 253:                     "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
 254:                     f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
 255:                     f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 256:                 )
 257:                 return PdfPageIndexEntry(
 258:                     page_number=page_number,
 259:                     topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
 260:                 )
 261: 
 262:     return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
 263: 
 264: 
 265: async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(  # 设计：并发执行整本 PDF 打标；功能：受限并发汇总全部页结果；默认保持页序，原因：便于直接落盘成索引。
 266:     pages: list[str],
 267:     company_name: str = "",
 268:     max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
 269: ) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
 270:     semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
 271:     total_pages = len(pages)
 272:     tasks = [
 273:         summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
 274:             page_number=page_number,
 275:             page_text=page_text,
 276:             company_name=company_name,
 277:             total_pages=total_pages,
 278:             semaphore=semaphore,
 279:         )
 280:         for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
 281:     ]
 282:     return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
 283: 
 284: 
 285: """并发页索引入口"""
 286: 
 287: 
 288: def ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel(  # 设计：并发页索引总入口；功能：优先读缓存再按需重建；可调：company_name、force_rebuild；默认空公司名且不强制重建，原因：兼容性更高。
 289:     pdf_file_path: str,
 290:     company_name: str = "",
 291:     force_rebuild: bool = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,
 292: ) -> str:
 293:     pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
 294:     if not pdf_path.exists():
 295:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")
 296: 
 297:     index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
 298:     if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
 299:         set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
 300:         return str(index_path)
 301: 
 302:     pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
 303:     max_concurrency = get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency()
 304:     print(
 305:         "[PDF Index Parallel] using bounded concurrency "
 306:         f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
 307:     )
 308:     page_entries = asyncio.run(
 309:         summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
 310:             pages=pages,
 311:             company_name=company_name,
 312:             max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
 313:         )
 314:     )
 315: 
 316:     payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
 317:     saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
 318:     set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
 319:     return saved_index_path
```

### 0082 ASSISTANT (commentary)

```text
发现了一个很具体的小问题：Windows 的 `Set-Content -Encoding UTF8` 给文件加了 BOM，Python 在最开头就把它当成非法字符了。我把它转成无 BOM UTF-8 再跑一次解析，这样结果才可信。
```

                          prepend an additional prefix to every line of output
    --no-prefix           do not show any source or destination prefix
    --default-prefix      use default prefixes a/ and b/
    --inter-hunk-context <n>
                          show context between diff hunks up to the specified number of lines
    --output-indicator-new <char>
                          specify the character to indicate a new line instead of '+'
    --output-indicator-old <char>
                          specify the character to indicate an old line instead of '-'
    --output-indicator-context <char>
                          specify the character to indicate a context instead of ' '

Diff rename options
    -B, --break-rewrites[=<n>[/<m>]]
                          break complete rewrite changes into pairs of delete and create
    -M, --find-renames[=<n>]
                          detect renames
    -D, --irreversible-delete
                          omit the preimage for deletes
    -C, --find-copies[=<n>]
                          detect copies
    --[no-]find-copies-harder
                          use unmodified files as source to find copies
    --no-renames          disable rename detection
    --[no-]rename-empty   use empty blobs as rename source
    --[no-]follow         continue listing the history of a file beyond renames
    -l <n>                prevent rename/copy detection if the number of rename/copy targets exceeds given limit

Diff algorithm options
    --minimal             produce the smallest possible diff
    -w, --ignore-all-space
                          ignore whitespace when comparing lines
    -b, --ignore-space-change
                          ignore changes in amount of whitespace
    --ignore-space-at-eol ignore changes in whitespace at EOL
    --ignore-cr-at-eol    ignore carrier-return at the end of line
    --ignore-blank-lines  ignore changes whose lines are all blank
    -I, --[no-]ignore-matching-lines <regex>
                          ignore changes whose all lines match <regex>
    --[no-]indent-heuristic
                          heuristic to shift diff hunk boundaries for easy reading
    --patience            generate diff using the "patience diff" algorithm
    --histogram           generate diff using the "histogram diff" algorithm
    --diff-algorithm <algorithm>
                          choose a diff algorithm
    --anchored <text>     generate diff using the "anchored diff" algorithm
    --word-diff[=<mode>]  show word diff, using <mode> to delimit changed words
    --word-diff-regex <regex>
                          use <regex> to decide what a word is
    --color-words[=<regex>]
                          equivalent to --word-diff=color --word-diff-regex=<regex>
    --[no-]color-moved[=<mode>]
                          moved lines of code are colored differently
    --[no-]color-moved-ws <mode>
                          how white spaces are ignored in --color-moved

Other diff options
    --[no-]relative[=<prefix>]
                          when run from subdir, exclude changes outside and show relative paths
    -a, --[no-]text       treat all files as text
    -R                    swap two inputs, reverse the diff
    --[no-]exit-code      exit with 1 if there were differences, 0 otherwise
    --[no-]quiet          disable all output of the program
    --[no-]ext-diff       allow an external diff helper to be executed
    --[no-]textconv       run external text conversion filters when comparing binary files
    --ignore-submodules[=<when>]
                          ignore changes to submodules in the diff generation
    --submodule[=<format>]
                          specify how differences in submodules are shown
    --ita-invisible-in-index
                          hide 'git add -N' entries from the index
    --ita-visible-in-index
                          treat 'git add -N' entries as real in the index
    -S <string>           look for differences that change the number of occurrences of the specified string
    -G <regex>            look for differences that change the number of occurrences of the specified regex
    --pickaxe-all         show all changes in the changeset with -S or -G
    --pickaxe-regex       treat <string> in -S as extended POSIX regular expression
    -O <file>             control the order in which files appear in the output
    --rotate-to <path>    show the change in the specified path first
    --skip-to <path>      skip the output to the specified path
    --find-object <object-id>
                          look for differences that change the number of occurrences of the specified object
    --diff-filter [(A|C|D|M|R|T|U|X|B)...[*]]
                          select files by diff type
    --output <file>       output to a specific file

```text
Exit code: 0
Wall time: 0.8 seconds
Output:
import os
from pathlib import Path
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from crewai import Agent, Crew, LLM, Process, Task
from crewai.project import CrewBase, agent, crew, task
from crewai_tools import SerperDevTool
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.MarkdownToPdfTool import (
    MarkdownToPdfTool,
)
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.pdf_page_tools import (
    ReadPdfPageIndexTool,
    ReadPdfPagesTool,
)
load_dotenv()


"""LLM 与 Crew 定义"""
PROJECT_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
PROJECT_LOG_DIR = PROJECT_ROOT / "logs"
DEFAULT_CREW_LOG_FILE = str(PROJECT_LOG_DIR / "crew_default.json")


def get_llm(  # 设计：统一 LLM 入口；功能：按流程覆写采样与容错；可调：temperature 常用 0-1、timeout>0/None、max_retries>=0/None；默认 0.5/60/1 兼顾稳定与响应速度。
    temperature: float = 0.5,
    timeout: float | int | None = 60,
    max_retries: int | None = 1,
) -> LLM:
    return LLM(
        api_base="https://openrouter.ai/api/v1",
        model="openrouter/google/gemini-3-flash-preview",
        api_key=os.getenv("OPENROUTER_API_KEY"),
        temperature=temperature,
        timeout=timeout,
        max_retries=max_retries,
    )

shared_search_tool = SerperDevTool()  # 设计：复用搜索实例；功能：补公开信息核验；默认全局共享以减少重复初始化。
shared_pdf_page_index_tool = ReadPdfPageIndexTool()  # 设计：统一筛页入口；功能：先读页索引再选页；默认全员共用以固定调用顺序。
shared_pdf_page_reader_tool = ReadPdfPagesTool()  # 设计：统一读页入口；功能：直读指定页文本；默认共用以避免重复实现。

@CrewBase
class AutomatedResearchReportGeneratorV01Crew:  # 设计：集中装配研究报告主流程；功能：把 YAML 配置映射为 agents、tasks 与 crew；默认顺序执行以保证上下游稳定。

    agents_config = "config/agents.yaml"
    tasks_config = "config/tasks.yaml"
    output_log_file_path: str | bool | None = DEFAULT_CREW_LOG_FILE

    @agent
    def industry_research_analyst(self) -> Agent:  # 设计：定义首个标准分析 agent；功能：行业研究并示范通用 agent 配置；默认低温度和禁委派以提高可控性。
        return Agent(
            config=self.agents_config["industry_research_analyst"],  # type: ignore[index]  # 默认读 YAML；可切换同结构配置；原因是角色文案与代码解耦。
            tools=[  # 可调：按任务增减工具；默认索引+读页+搜索，原因是行业研究同时需要文档定位与外部核验。
                shared_pdf_page_index_tool,
                shared_pdf_page_reader_tool,
                shared_search_tool,
            ],
            llm=get_llm(temperature=0.3),  # 可调：temperature 常用 0-1；默认 0.3，原因是分析要稳但仍保留少量归纳弹性。
            function_calling_llm=None,  # 可调：独立工具调用模型/None；默认 None，原因是沿用主模型便于维护。
            max_iter=25,  # 可调：建议 >=1；默认 25，原因是给复杂任务足够迭代空间。
            max_rpm=None,  # 可调：正整数/None；默认 None，原因是先不做人为限流。
            max_execution_time=None,  # 可调：秒数/None；默认 None，原因是交给上层超时控制。
            verbose=True,  # 可调：True/False；默认 True，原因是当前阶段更重视可观测性。
            allow_delegation=False,  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因是角色边界已明确。
            step_callback=None,  # 可调：回调函数/None；默认 None，原因是暂不插入额外钩子。
            cache=True,  # 可调：True/False；默认 True，原因是减少重复调用成本。
            allow_code_execution=False,  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因是当前任务以阅读分析为主。
            max_retry_limit=2,  # 可调：建议 >=0；默认 2，原因是兼顾重试收益与耗时。
            respect_context_window=True,  # 可调：True/False；默认 True，原因是避免长上下文溢出。
            use_system_prompt=True,  # 可调：True/False；默认 True，原因是保留系统约束。
            reasoning=False,  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因是此流程更依赖显式任务拆分。
            max_reasoning_attempts=5,  # 可调：建议 >=1/None；默认 5，原因是与 reasoning 兼容保留上限。
            inject_date=True,  # 可调：True/False；默认 True，原因是搜索与时效判断需要日期上下文。
        )

    @agent
    def business_model_analyst(self) -> Agent:  # 设计：聚焦商业模式；功能：只读 PDF 内部证据；默认不挂搜索以减少外部噪声。
        return Agent(
            config=self.agents_config["business_model_analyst"],  # type: ignore[index]
            tools=[shared_pdf_page_index_tool, shared_pdf_page_reader_tool],
            llm=get_llm(temperature=0.3),
            function_calling_llm=None,
            max_iter=25,
            max_rpm=None,
            max_execution_time=None,
            verbose=True,
            allow_delegation=False,
            step_callback=None,
            cache=True,
            allow_code_execution=False,
            max_retry_limit=2,
            respect_context_window=True,
            use_system_prompt=True,
            reasoning=False,
            max_reasoning_attempts=None,
            inject_date=True,
        )

    @agent
    def financial_analysis_specialist(self) -> Agent:  # 设计：聚焦财务分析；功能：从原文抽取并归纳财务结论；默认低温度以压缩主观波动。
        return Agent(
            config=self.agents_config["financial_analysis_specialist"],  # type: ignore[index]
            tools=[shared_pdf_page_index_tool, shared_pdf_page_reader_tool],
            llm=get_llm(temperature=0.3),
            function_calling_llm=None,
            max_iter=25,
            max_rpm=None,
            max_execution_time=None,
            verbose=True,
            allow_delegation=False,
            step_callback=None,
            cache=True,
            allow_code_execution=False,
            max_retry_limit=2,
            respect_context_window=True,
            use_system_prompt=True,
            reasoning=False,
            max_reasoning_attempts=None,
            inject_date=True,
        )
```

  45: class ParallelPageTopicSummary(BaseModel):  # 璁捐锛氬畾涔夊崟椤电粨鏋勫寲杈撳嚭锛涘姛鑳斤細鍙繚鐣?topic锛涢粯璁ゆ渶灏忓瓧娈甸泦渚夸簬绋冲畾瑙ｆ瀽銆?    topic: str = Field(..., description="褰撳墠椤电殑绠€鐭富棰樻爣绛?)
  46:

  48: """骞跺彂椤电储寮曡緟鍔╁嚱鏁?""
  49: 
  50: 
  51: def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 璁捐锛氱粺涓€娓呮礂涓婚锛涘姛鑳斤細鍘嬫垚绋冲畾鐭爣绛撅紱榛樿瓒呴暱鎴柇涓旂┖鍊煎洖閫€锛屽師鍥狅細渚夸簬绛涢〉涓庡睍绀恒€?    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
  52:     normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
  53:     compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
  54:     if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
  55:         normalized = ""
  56:     if not normalized:
  57:         normalized = fallback
  58:     return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]
  59: 
  60: 
  61: def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 璁捐锛氬厹搴曠敓鎴愪富棰橈紱鍔熻兘锛氬け璐ユ椂鍙栭涓儚鏍囬鐨勬枃鏈紱榛樿鍥為€€ fallback锛屽師鍥狅細绱㈠紩娴佺▼涓嶈兘涓柇銆?    for line in page_text.splitlines():
  62:         cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
  63:         if len(cleaned) >= 2:
  64:             return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
  65:     return fallback
  66: 
  67: 
  68: def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 璁捐锛氬吋瀹瑰厹搴曡В鏋愶紱鍔熻兘锛氫粠 raw 涓彁鍙?topic锛涢粯璁ゅ紓甯告椂杩斿洖鍘熸枃鎴栫┖涓诧紝鍘熷洜锛氬悗缁繕浼氬啀娓呮礂銆?    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
  69:     if not cleaned:
  70:         return ""
  71: 
  72:     if cleaned.startswith("```"):
  73:         cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
  74:         if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
  75:             cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()
  76: 
  77:     try:
  78:         data = json.loads(cleaned)
  79:     except Exception:
  80:         return cleaned
  81: 
  82:     if isinstance(data, dict):
  83:         return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
  84:     return ""
  85: 
  86: 
  87: def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 璁捐锛氱粺涓€瑙ｆ瀽 LiteAgent 杈撳嚭锛涘姛鑳斤細浼樺厛璇荤粨鏋勫寲瀛楁锛屽け璐ュ啀璇?raw锛涘師鍥狅細鍏煎涓嶅悓杩斿洖褰㈡€併€?    topic = ""
  88:     if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
  89:         topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
  90:     if not topic:
  91:         topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
  92:     return topic
  93: 
  94: 
  95: def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 璁捐锛氳鍙栨暣鍨嬬幆澧冨彉閲忥紱鍔熻兘锛氱粰骞跺彂鍜岄噸璇曞弬鏁扮暀杩愯鏃跺紑鍏筹紱榛樿闈炴硶鍊煎洖閫€榛樿鍊硷紝鍘熷洜锛氬噺灏戦厤缃敊璇奖鍝嶃€?    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
  96:     if not raw:
  97:         return default
  98: 
  99:     try:
 100:         return max(minimum, int(raw))
 101:     except ValueError:
 102:         return default
 103: 
 104: 
 105: def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 璁捐锛氭毚闇插苟鍙戝害閰嶇疆锛涘姛鑳斤細缁熶竴浠庣幆澧冨彉閲忚鍙栵紱榛樿鍥為€€甯搁噺锛屽師鍥狅細渚夸簬閮ㄧ讲渚ц皟浼樸€?    return _read_int_env(
 106:         "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
 107:         PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
 108:         minimum=1,
 109:     )
 110: 
 111: 
 112: def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 璁捐锛氭毚闇查噸璇曟鏁伴厤缃紱鍔熻兘锛氱粺涓€浠庣幆澧冨彉閲忚鍙栵紱榛樿鍥為€€甯搁噺锛屽師鍥狅細渚夸簬鎸夋ā鍨嬬ǔ瀹氭€ц皟浼樸€?    return _read_int_env(
 113:         "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
 114:         PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
 115:         minimum=0,
 116:     )
 117: 
 118: 
 119: def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 璁捐锛氳瘑鍒彲閲嶈瘯閿欒锛涘姛鑳斤細鍙闄愭祦鍜屼复鏃舵晠闅滈噸璇曪紱鍘熷洜锛氶伩鍏嶅纭畾鎬ч敊璇棤鎰忎箟閲嶆斁銆?    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
 120:     retryable_markers = (
 121:         "429",
 122:         "rate limit",
 123:         "too many requests",
 124:         "timeout",
 125:         "timed out",
 126:         "connection",
 127:         "temporarily unavailable",
 128:         "bad gateway",
 129:         "gateway timeout",
 130:         "service unavailable",
 131:         "502",
 132:         "503",
 133:         "504",
 134:     )
 135:     return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)
 136: 
 137: 
 138: def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 璁捐锛氶泦涓粍瑁呭崟椤?prompt锛涘姛鑳斤細鎷艰鍒欍€侀〉鐮佸拰椤垫枃锛涢粯璁?company_name 涓虹┖锛屽師鍥狅細鍏煎涓婃父鏈瘑鍒叕鍙稿悕銆?    prompt_parts = [
 139:         "浣犳槸涓€涓姇琛屽垵绾у垎鏋愬笀锛岃礋璐ｇ粰涓€椤?PDF 鎵撲竴涓畝鐭富棰樻爣绛俱€?,
 140:         "",
 141:         "瑙勫垯锛?,
 142:     ]
 143:     prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
 144:     prompt_parts.extend(
 145:         [
 146:             "",
 147:             f"鍏徃鍚嶇О锛歿company_name or PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
 148:             f"椤电爜锛歿page_number}",
 149:             f"褰撳墠椤垫枃鏈細{page_text}",
 150:         ]
 151:     )
 152:     return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()
 153: 
 154: 
 155: """骞跺彂椤电储寮?Agent"""
 156: 
 157: 
 158: def create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent() -> LiteAgent:  # 璁捐锛氱嫭绔嬪垱寤哄苟鍙戠储寮?agent锛涘姛鑳斤細涓烘瘡涓紓姝ヤ换鍔℃彁渚涜交閲忓崟椤垫墽琛屽櫒锛涢粯璁ゅ揩澶辫触閰嶇疆锛屽師鍥狅細棰勫鐞嗗簲灏藉揩鍥為€€銆?    return LiteAgent(
 159:         role=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,
 160:         goal=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,
 161:         backstory=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,
 162:         llm=get_llm(
 163:             temperature=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
 164:             timeout=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 165:             max_retries=0,
 166:         ),
 167:         verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
 168:         max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
 169:         response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
 170:     )
 171: 
 172: 
 173: """骞跺彂椤电储寮曟墽琛?""
 174: 
 175: 
 176: async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(  # 璁捐锛氭墽琛屽崟椤靛紓姝ユ墦鏍囷紱鍔熻兘锛氳繑鍥為〉鐮佷笌涓婚鏄犲皠锛涢粯璁ょ┖椤电洿杩斿浐瀹氭爣绛撅紝鍘熷洜锛氶伩鍏嶆棤鏁堣皟鐢ㄣ€?    page_number: int,
 177:     page_text: str,
 178:     company_name: str,
 179:     total_pages: int,
 180:     semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
 181: ) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
 182:     fallback = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"绗瑊page_number}椤?
 183:     if not page_text.strip():
 184:         return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
 185: 
 186:     prompt = build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
 187:         page_number=page_number,
 188:         page_text=page_text,
 189:         company_name=company_name,
 190:     )
 191:     retry_limit = get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit()
 192: 
 193:     async with semaphore:
 194:         for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
 195:             started_at = perf_counter()
 196:             try:
 197:                 result = await create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent().kickoff_async(
 198:                     prompt,
 199:                     response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
 200:                 )
 201:                 topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
 202:                 elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 203:                 print(
 204:                     f"[PDF Index Parallel] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
 205:                     f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
 206:                 )
 207:                 return PdfPageIndexEntry(
 208:                     page_number=page_number,
 209:                     topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
 210:                 )
 211:             except Exception as exc:
 212:                 elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
 213:                 should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
 214:                 if should_retry:
 215:                     delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
 216:                     print(
 217:                         "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
 218:                         f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
 219:                         f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
 220:                         f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
 221:                         f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
 222:                     )
 223:                     await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
 224:                     continue
 225: 
 226:                 print(
 227:                     "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
 228:                     f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
 229:                     f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
 230:                 )
 231:                 return PdfPageIndexEntry(
 232:                     page_number=page_number,
 233:                     topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
 234:                 )
 235: 
 236:     return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)
 237: 
 238: 
 239: async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(  # 璁捐锛氬苟鍙戞墽琛屾暣鏈?PDF 鎵撴爣锛涘姛鑳斤細鍙楅檺骞跺彂姹囨€诲叏閮ㄩ〉缁撴灉锛涢粯璁や繚鎸侀〉搴忥紝鍘熷洜锛氫究浜庣洿鎺ヨ惤鐩樻垚绱㈠紩銆?    pages: list[str],
 240:     company_name: str = "",
 241:     max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
 242: ) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
 243:     semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
 244:     total_pages = len(pages)
 245:     tasks = [
 246:         summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
 247:             page_number=page_number,
 248:             page_text=page_text,
 249:             company_name=company_name,
 250:             total_pages=total_pages,
 251:             semaphore=semaphore,
 252:         )
 253:         for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
 254:     ]
 255:     return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
 256: 
 257: 
 258: """骞跺彂椤电储寮曞叆鍙?""
 259: 
 260: 
 261: def ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel(  # 璁捐锛氬苟鍙戦〉绱㈠紩鎬诲叆鍙ｏ紱鍔熻兘锛氫紭鍏堣缂撳瓨鍐嶆寜闇€閲嶅缓锛涘彲璋冿細company_name銆乫orce_rebuild锛涢粯璁ょ┖鍏徃鍚嶄笖涓嶅己鍒堕噸寤猴紝鍘熷洜锛氬吋瀹规€ф洿楂樸€?    pdf_file_path: str,
 262:     company_name: str = "",
 263:     force_rebuild: bool = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,
 264: ) -> str:
 265:     pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
 266:     if not pdf_path.exists():
 267:         raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")
 268: 
 269:     index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
 270:     if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
 271:         set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
 272:         return str(index_path)
 273: 
 274:     pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
 275:     max_concurrency = get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency()
 276:     print(
 277:         "[PDF Index Parallel] using bounded concurrency "
 278:         f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
 279:     )
 280:     page_entries = asyncio.run(
 281:         summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
 282:             pages=pages,
 283:             company_name=company_name,
 284:             max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
 285:         )
 286:     )
 287: 
 288:     payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
 289:     saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
 290:     set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
 291:     return saved_index_path
```
### 0142 ASSISTANT (final_answer)

```text
我已经加了测试脚本 [`test_pdf_indexing_parallel.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/test_pdf_indexing_parallel.py)。它做了两类验证：

- `mock` 模式：不依赖外网模型，直接验证并发上限、空白页处理、索引 JSON 落盘、缓存复用。
- `live` 模式：走真实 `LiteAgent`，可以对真实 PDF 做冒烟测试。

我自己已经跑通了 `mock` 模式，结果是通过的：4 页样例 PDF 成功生成索引，topic 为 `overview / finance / 空白页 / risk`，非空白页触发了 3 次 agent 调用，并发峰值是 2，说明 [`pdf_indexing_parellel.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py) 的 `Semaphore` 控制和缓存逻辑都正常。

你可以这样跑：

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH='C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\src'
& "C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\.venv\Scripts\python.exe" "C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\test_pdf_indexing_parallel.py" --mode mock --max-concurrency 2
```

如果要真跑模型：

```powershell
$env:PYTHONPATH='C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\src'
& "C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\.venv\Scripts\python.exe" "C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\test_pdf_indexing_parallel.py" --mode live --pdf "C:\PyProjects\automated_research_report_generator_v0.1\pdf\sehk26022601053_c.pdf" --max-concurrency 2
```

### 0152 ASSISTANT (commentary)

```text
刚才那次是真实全书跑了，但命中的是外网连接失败，不是脚本逻辑失败：388 页的任务已经开始分发，随后每页都在 `ConnectionError` 上重试和回退，所以才拖到超时。按照这个环境规则，我接下来会直接申请一次脱离沙箱的网络运行，再用同一本 PDF 重新完整跑完。
```

### 0155 ASSISTANT (final_answer)

```text
我直接拿项目里的 [`sehk26033003882_c.pdf`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/pdf/sehk26033003882_c.pdf) 跑了整本，并发度是 `4`。

结果先说结论：能产出完整页索引，但当前并发版并没有“顺利用 LiteAgent 成功返回结构化结果”，而是几乎全程走了异常兜底。

本次实测数据：
- PDF 页数：`388`
- 总耗时：`617.852s`，大约 `10分18秒`
- 输出索引：[`sehk26033003882_c_page_index.json`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/.cache/pdf_page_indexes/sehk26033003882_c_page_index.json)
- 吞吐大约：`37.7 页/分钟`

索引确实生成出来了，前后页 topic 也看起来“像能用”：
- 前几页：`香港聯合交易所有限公`、`重要提示：您如對本文`、`編纂`、`致投資者的重要通知`
- 中间页：`管理與控制存貨的能力`、`收益`、`按銷售渠道劃分的提供`
- 末尾页：`免責聲明`、`專家資格`、`送呈香港公司註冊處處`

但关键问题也很明显：
- 在 [`pdf_indexing_parellel.py`](/C:/PyProjects/automated_research_report_generator_v0.1/src/automated_research_report_generator_v0_1/pdf_indexing_parellel.py) 的 `kickoff_async(..., response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary)` 这条路径上，CrewAI 事件层反复报 `ValidationError`。
- 报错核心是：`LiteAgentExecutionCompletedEvent.output` 期望是 `string`，但拿到的是 `ParallelPageTopicSummary(...)` 这种 Pydantic 对象。
- 所以日志里几乎每页都是 `failed after ... with ValidationError`，然后被你的 `_heuristic_topic(...)` 兜底接住，最终还是写出了索引。

另外还有次要问题：
- 控制台编码是 `gbk`，CrewAI 事件里有 emoji，导致一堆 `gbk codec can't encode character` 的噪声日志。
- 后段还混进了少量真实网络错误/超时，但因为有 fallback，所以整体没中断。

所以这次真实测试给出的判断是：

1. 当前脚本“可用”  
它能在大 PDF 上完整跑完，并生成一份可读的页索引。

2. 但“没有按设计方式成功工作”  
主路径本来应该是 LiteAgent 成功返回结构化 `topic`；现在实际主要靠异常后的启发式首行提取在工作。

3. 现在的索引质量更接近“页面首行标签”，而不是“LLM 生成的稳定短主题标签”  
从结果看，很多页 topic 就是首行截断后的文本，这和你的 fallback 逻辑一致。

如果你愿意，我下一步建议直接修这个根因：把并发版改成一个不会触发 `LiteAgentExecutionCompletedEvent.output` 校验错误的返回路径，再重新对这本 388 页 PDF 跑一次，看看真实 LLM 成功率和耗时会变成什么样。
```

```

```text
Exit code: 0
Wall time: 0.8 seconds
Output:
from __future__ import annotations

import asyncio
import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from time import perf_counter

from crewai.lite_agent import LiteAgent
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field

from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.crew import get_llm
from automated_research_report_generator_v0_1.tools.pdf_page_tools import (
    PdfPageIndexEntry,
    build_page_index_payload,
    default_page_index_path,
    extract_pdf_pages,
    page_index_is_current,
    save_page_index,
    set_pdf_context,
)

"""并发版 PDF 逐页索引"""

"""并发页索引 Agent 参数"""

PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE = "PDF 并发逐页索引专员"  # 默认角色名；功能：限定 agent 只做逐页打标；原因：避免提前跨页分析。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL = (  # 默认目标；功能：为后续 agent 提供筛页标签；原因：减少全文盲读。
    "并发读取 PDF 页面，并为每一页生成一个简短主题标签，帮助后续 agent 快速定位相关页。"
)
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY = (  # 默认背景；功能：强化单页视角；原因：防止越界总结整份文档。
    "你专门负责按页阅读 PDF。你不会跨页总结，也不会提前做整份文档分析。"
    "你的唯一职责是只根据当前这一页的内容，输出一个非常短、便于筛页的主题标签。"
)
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE = 0.1  # 可调：常用 0-0.3；默认 0.1，原因：标签更稳更短。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE = False  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因：并发执行时避免日志过多。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS = 20  # 可调：建议 >0；默认 20，原因：单页调用不应长时间阻塞。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT = 4  # 可调：建议 1-8；默认 4，原因：在吞吐和限流风险之间折中。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT = 2  # 可调：建议 >=0；默认 2，原因：预处理容忍短暂波动但不无限重试。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS = 2.0  # 可调：建议 >0；默认 2 秒，原因：给限流或瞬时故障留恢复时间。

"""并发页索引任务参数"""

PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS = 10  # 可调：建议 4-15；默认 10，原因：既短又够区分主题。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY = "未知公司"  # 默认公司占位；功能：补齐 prompt 上下文；原因：上游可能识别失败。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC = "空白页"  # 默认空白页标签；功能：显式标记无文本页；原因：避免误判异常。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT = False  # 可调：True/False；默认 False，原因：优先复用缓存。
PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES = (  # 默认规则集；功能：约束标签长度和口径；原因：后续筛页更稳定。
    "只输出一个 `topic` 字段。",
    f"`topic` 最多 {PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS} 个字。",
    "只关注当前这一页，不要总结整份文档。",
    "尽量使用具体的业务主题，不要使用空泛表述。",
    "如果本页主要是表格，就概括表格的主题。",
    "如果本页难以判断，就返回一个谨慎、简短的主题。",
    "不要输出解释、前后缀、Markdown 代码块或额外文本。",
)


class ParallelPageTopicSummary(BaseModel):  # 设计：定义单页结构化输出；功能：只保留 topic；默认最小字段集便于稳定解析。
    topic: str = Field(..., description="当前页的简短主题标签")


"""并发页索引辅助函数"""


def _normalize_topic(topic: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：统一清洗主题；功能：压成稳定短标签；默认超长截断且空值回退，原因：便于筛页与展示。
    normalized = " ".join((topic or "").split())
    normalized = normalized.replace('"', "").replace("'", "").replace("`", "").strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
    compact = normalized.replace(" ", "").lower()
    if compact in {"json", "{", "}", "topic", "none", "null"}:
        normalized = ""
    if not normalized:
        normalized = fallback
    return normalized[:PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_TOPIC_MAX_CHARS]


def _heuristic_topic(page_text: str, fallback: str) -> str:  # 设计：兜底生成主题；功能：失败时取首个像标题的文本；默认回退 fallback，原因：索引流程不能中断。
    for line in page_text.splitlines():
        cleaned = " ".join(line.split()).strip(" ,.;:()[]{}")
        if len(cleaned) >= 2:
            return _normalize_topic(cleaned, fallback)
    return fallback


def _extract_topic_from_raw(raw: str) -> str:  # 设计：兼容兜底解析；功能：从 raw 中提取 topic；默认异常时返回原文或空串，原因：后续还会再清洗。
    cleaned = (raw or "").strip()
    if not cleaned:
        return ""

    if cleaned.startswith("```"):
        cleaned = cleaned.strip("`").strip()
        if cleaned.lower().startswith("json"):
            cleaned = cleaned[4:].strip()

    try:
        data = json.loads(cleaned)
    except Exception:
        return cleaned

    if isinstance(data, dict):
        return str(data.get("topic", "") or "")
    return ""


def _extract_topic_from_result(result: object) -> str:  # 设计：统一解析 LiteAgent 输出；功能：优先读结构化字段，失败再读 raw；原因：兼容不同返回形态。
    topic = ""
    if getattr(result, "pydantic", None):
        topic = str(result.pydantic.topic or "")
    if not topic:
        topic = _extract_topic_from_raw(getattr(result, "raw", "") or "")
    return topic


def _read_int_env(name: str, default: int, minimum: int = 1) -> int:  # 设计：读取整型环境变量；功能：给并发和重试参数留运行时开关；默认非法值回退默认值，原因：减少配置错误影响。
    raw = os.getenv(name, "").strip()
    if not raw:
        return default

    try:
        return max(minimum, int(raw))
    except ValueError:
        return default


def get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency() -> int:  # 设计：暴露并发度配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于部署侧调优。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_MAX_CONCURRENCY",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
        minimum=1,
    )


def get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit() -> int:  # 设计：暴露重试次数配置；功能：统一从环境变量读取；默认回退常量，原因：便于按模型稳定性调优。
    return _read_int_env(
        "PDF_INDEX_PARALLEL_RETRY_LIMIT",
        PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_LIMIT_DEFAULT,
        minimum=0,
    )


def _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:  # 设计：识别可重试错误；功能：只对限流和临时故障重试；原因：避免对确定性错误无意义重放。
    error_text = f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}".lower()
    retryable_markers = (
        "429",
        "rate limit",
        "too many requests",
        "timeout",
        "timed out",
        "connection",
        "temporarily unavailable",
        "bad gateway",
        "gateway timeout",
        "service unavailable",
        "502",
        "503",
        "504",
    )
    return any(marker in error_text for marker in retryable_markers)


def build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(page_number: int, page_text: str, company_name: str = "") -> str:  # 设计：集中组装单页 prompt；功能：拼规则、页码和页文；默认 company_name 为空，原因：兼容上游未识别公司名。
    prompt_parts = [
        "你是一个投行初级分析师，负责给一页 PDF 打一个简短主题标签。",
        "",
        "规则：",
    ]
    prompt_parts.extend(f"- {rule}" for rule in PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_PROMPT_RULES)
    prompt_parts.extend(
        [
            "",
            f"公司名称：{company_name or PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_UNKNOWN_COMPANY}",
            f"页码：{page_number}",
            f"当前页文本：{page_text}",
        ]
    )
    return "\n".join(prompt_parts).strip()


"""并发页索引 Agent"""


def create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent() -> LiteAgent:  # 设计：独立创建并发索引 agent；功能：为每个异步任务提供轻量单页执行器；默认快失败配置，原因：预处理应尽快回退。
    return LiteAgent(
        role=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_ROLE,
        goal=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_GOAL,
        backstory=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_BACKSTORY,
        llm=get_llm(
            temperature=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TEMPERATURE,
            timeout=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
            max_retries=0,
        ),
        verbose=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_VERBOSE,
        max_execution_time=PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_AGENT_TIMEOUT_SECONDS,
        response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
    )


"""并发页索引执行"""


async def summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(  # 设计：执行单页异步打标；功能：返回页码与主题映射；默认空页直返固定标签，原因：避免无效调用。
    page_number: int,
    page_text: str,
    company_name: str,
    total_pages: int,
    semaphore: asyncio.Semaphore,
) -> PdfPageIndexEntry:
    fallback = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_EMPTY_PAGE_TOPIC if not page_text.strip() else f"第{page_number}页"
    if not page_text.strip():
        return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)

    prompt = build_parallel_page_topic_task_prompt(
        page_number=page_number,
        page_text=page_text,
        company_name=company_name,
    )
    retry_limit = get_parallel_page_index_retry_limit()

    async with semaphore:
        for attempt in range(retry_limit + 1):
            started_at = perf_counter()
            try:
                result = await create_parallel_page_indexer_lite_agent().kickoff_async(
                    prompt,
                    response_format=ParallelPageTopicSummary,
                )
                topic = _extract_topic_from_result(result)
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                print(
                    f"[PDF Index Parallel] page {page_number}/{total_pages} "
                    f"completed in {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_normalize_topic(str(topic), fallback),
                )
            except Exception as exc:
                elapsed_seconds = perf_counter() - started_at
                should_retry = attempt < retry_limit and _is_retryable_page_index_error(exc)
                if should_retry:
                    delay_seconds = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_RETRY_BASE_DELAY_SECONDS * (2 ** attempt)
                    print(
                        "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                        f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                        f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}. "
                        f"Retrying in {delay_seconds:.1f}s "
                        f"({attempt + 1}/{retry_limit})"
                    )
                    await asyncio.sleep(delay_seconds)
                    continue

                print(
                    "[PDF Index Parallel] page "
                    f"{page_number}/{total_pages} failed after {elapsed_seconds:.1f}s with "
                    f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"
                )
                return PdfPageIndexEntry(
                    page_number=page_number,
                    topic=_heuristic_topic(page_text, fallback),
                )

    return PdfPageIndexEntry(page_number=page_number, topic=fallback)


async def summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(  # 设计：并发执行整本 PDF 打标；功能：受限并发汇总全部页结果；默认保持页序，原因：便于直接落盘成索引。
    pages: list[str],
    company_name: str = "",
    max_concurrency: int = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_MAX_CONCURRENCY_DEFAULT,
) -> list[PdfPageIndexEntry]:
    semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrency)
    total_pages = len(pages)
    tasks = [
        summarize_page_topic_with_lite_agent_async(
            page_number=page_number,
            page_text=page_text,
            company_name=company_name,
            total_pages=total_pages,
            semaphore=semaphore,
        )
        for page_number, page_text in enumerate(pages, start=1)
    ]
    return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)


"""并发页索引入口"""


def ensure_pdf_page_index_parallel(  # 设计：并发页索引总入口；功能：优先读缓存再按需重建；可调：company_name、force_rebuild；默认空公司名且不强制重建，原因：兼容性更高。
    pdf_file_path: str,
    company_name: str = "",
    force_rebuild: bool = PARALLEL_PAGE_INDEX_FORCE_REBUILD_DEFAULT,
) -> str:
    pdf_path = Path(pdf_file_path).expanduser().resolve()
    if not pdf_path.exists():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"PDF file does not exist: {pdf_path}")

    index_path = default_page_index_path(pdf_path)
    if not force_rebuild and page_index_is_current(pdf_path, index_path):
        set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), str(index_path))
        return str(index_path)

    pages = extract_pdf_pages(pdf_path)
    max_concurrency = get_parallel_page_index_max_concurrency()
    print(
        "[PDF Index Parallel] using bounded concurrency "
        f"(max_concurrency={max_concurrency}, pages={len(pages)})"
    )
    page_entries = asyncio.run(
        summarize_pages_with_parallel_lite_agent(
            pages=pages,
            company_name=company_name,
            max_concurrency=max_concurrency,
        )
    )

    payload = build_page_index_payload(pdf_path, page_entries)
    saved_index_path = save_page_index(payload, index_path)
    set_pdf_context(str(pdf_path), saved_index_path)
    return saved_index_path
```

def _kickoff_with_a2a_support(
    agent: LiteAgent,
    original_kickoff: Callable[..., LiteAgentOutput],
    messages: str | list[LLMMessage],
    response_format: type[BaseModel] | None,
    input_files: dict[str, FileInput] | None,
    extension_registry: Any,
) -> LiteAgentOutput:
    """Wrap kickoff with A2A delegation using Task adapter.

    Args:
        agent: The LiteAgent instance.
        original_kickoff: The original kickoff method.
        messages: Input messages.
        response_format: Optional response format.
        input_files: Optional input files.
        extension_registry: A2A extension registry.

    Returns:
        LiteAgentOutput from either local execution or A2A delegation.
    """
    from crewai.a2a.utils.response_model import get_a2a_agents_and_response_model
    from crewai.a2a.wrapper import _execute_task_with_a2a
    from crewai.task import Task

    a2a_agents, agent_response_model = get_a2a_agents_and_response_model(agent.a2a)

    if not a2a_agents:
        return original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)

    if isinstance(messages, str):
        description = messages
    else:
        content = next(
            (m["content"] for m in reversed(messages) if m["role"] == "user"),
            None,
        )
        description = content if isinstance(content, str) else ""

    if not description:
        return original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)

    fake_task = Task(
        description=description,
        agent=agent,
        expected_output="Result from A2A delegation",
        input_files=input_files or {},
    )

    def task_to_kickoff_adapter(
        self: Any, task: Task, context: str | None, tools: list[Any] | None
    ) -> str:
        result = original_kickoff(messages, response_format, input_files)
        return result.raw

    result_str = _execute_task_with_a2a(
        self=agent,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
        a2a_agents=a2a_agents,
        original_fn=task_to_kickoff_adapter,
        task=fake_task,
        agent_response_model=agent_response_model,
        context=None,
        tools=None,
        extension_registry=extension_registry,
    )

    return LiteAgentOutput(
        raw=result_str,
        pydantic=None,
        agent_role=agent.role,
        usage_metrics=None,
        messages=[],
    )


class LiteAgent(FlowTrackable, BaseModel):
    """
    A lightweight agent that can process messages and use tools.

    .. deprecated::
        LiteAgent is deprecated and will be removed in a future version.
        Use ``Agent().kickoff(messages)`` instead, which provides the same
        functionality with additional features like memory and knowledge support.

    This agent is simpler than the full Agent class, focusing on direct execution
    rather than task delegation. It's designed to be used for simple interactions
    where a full crew is not needed.

    Attributes:
        role: The role of the agent.
        goal: The objective of the agent.
        backstory: The backstory of the agent.
        llm: The language model that will run the agent.
        tools: Tools at the agent's disposal.
        verbose: Whether the agent execution should be in verbose mode.
        max_iterations: Maximum number of iterations for tool usage.
        max_execution_time: Maximum execution time in seconds.
        response_format: Optional Pydantic model for structured output.
    """

    model_config = {"arbitrary_types_allowed": True}
    id: UUID4 = Field(default_factory=uuid.uuid4, frozen=True)
    role: str = Field(description="Role of the agent")
    goal: str = Field(description="Goal of the agent")
    backstory: str = Field(description="Backstory of the agent")
    llm: str | InstanceOf[BaseLLM] | Any | None = Field(
        default=None, description="Language model that will run the agent"
    )
    tools: list[BaseTool] = Field(
        default_factory=list, description="Tools at agent's disposal"
    )
    max_iterations: int = Field(
        default=15, description="Maximum number of iterations for tool usage"
    )
    max_execution_time: int | None = Field(
        default=None, description=". Maximum execution time in seconds"
    )
    respect_context_window: bool = Field(
        default=True,
        description="Whether to respect the context window of the LLM",
    )
    use_stop_words: bool = Field(
        default=True,
        description="Whether to use stop words to prevent the LLM from using tools",
    )
    request_within_rpm_limit: Callable[[], bool] | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="Callback to check if the request is within the RPM8 limit",
    )
    i18n: I18N = Field(
        default_factory=get_i18n, description="Internationalization settings."
    )
    response_format: type[BaseModel] | None = Field(
        default=None, description="Pydantic model for structured output"
    )
    verbose: bool = Field(
        default=False, description="Whether to print execution details"
    )
    guardrail: GuardrailType | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="Function or string description of a guardrail to validate agent output",
    )
    guardrail_max_retries: int = Field(
        default=3, description="Maximum number of retries when guardrail fails"
    )
    a2a: (
        list[A2AConfig | A2AServerConfig | A2AClientConfig]
        | A2AConfig
        | A2AServerConfig
        | A2AClientConfig
        | None
    ) = Field(
        default=None,
        description="A2A (Agent-to-Agent) configuration for delegating tasks to remote agents. "
        "Can be a single A2AConfig/A2AClientConfig/A2AServerConfig, or a list of configurations.",
    )
    memory: bool | Any | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="If True, use default Memory(). If Memory/MemoryScope/MemorySlice, use it for recall and remember.",
```

"""Agent-related events moved to break circular dependencies."""

from __future__ import annotations

from collections.abc import Sequence
from typing import Any

from pydantic import ConfigDict, model_validator
from typing_extensions import Self

from crewai.agents.agent_builder.base_agent import BaseAgent
from crewai.events.base_events import BaseEvent
from crewai.tools.base_tool import BaseTool
from crewai.tools.structured_tool import CrewStructuredTool


class AgentExecutionStartedEvent(BaseEvent):
    """Event emitted when an agent starts executing a task"""

    agent: BaseAgent
    task: Any
    tools: Sequence[BaseTool | CrewStructuredTool] | None
    task_prompt: str
    type: str = "agent_execution_started"

    model_config = ConfigDict(arbitrary_types_allowed=True)

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def set_fingerprint_data(self) -> Self:
        """Set fingerprint data from the agent if available."""
        _set_agent_fingerprint(self, self.agent)
        return self


class AgentExecutionCompletedEvent(BaseEvent):
    """Event emitted when an agent completes executing a task"""

    agent: BaseAgent
    task: Any
    output: str
    type: str = "agent_execution_completed"

    model_config = ConfigDict(arbitrary_types_allowed=True)

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def set_fingerprint_data(self) -> Self:
        """Set fingerprint data from the agent if available."""
        _set_agent_fingerprint(self, self.agent)
        return self


class AgentExecutionErrorEvent(BaseEvent):
    """Event emitted when an agent encounters an error during execution"""

    agent: BaseAgent
    task: Any
    error: str
    type: str = "agent_execution_error"

    model_config = ConfigDict(arbitrary_types_allowed=True)

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def set_fingerprint_data(self) -> Self:
        """Set fingerprint data from the agent if available."""
        _set_agent_fingerprint(self, self.agent)
        return self

    messages: str | list[dict[str, str]]
    type: str = "lite_agent_execution_started"

    type: str = "agent_evaluation_failed"


def _set_agent_fingerprint(event: BaseEvent, agent: BaseAgent) -> None:
    """Set fingerprint data on an event from an agent object."""
    fp = agent.security_config.fingerprint
    if fp is not None:
        event.source_fingerprint = fp.uuid_str
        event.source_type = "agent"
        if fp.metadata:
            event.fingerprint_metadata = fp.metadata
